Quarrel Over Living Expenses - Legal Wife Angered and Sues

He Jingrong, from Nanhai, Guangdong, married Ye Ruizhen, also from the same hometown, seventeen years ago. They have three children together. However, eight years ago, He began a relationship with Li Qunfang. Since then, the legal wife has lived with her children in a separate residence at No. 23, Kejian Lane, Jiaxing Road, while he lives with his concubine at No. 35, Shishan Lane, Dongxi Huade Road. He runs a clothing business in Shanghai and is financially comfortable. Although the wife and concubine live separately, he still bears the living expenses for both sides, giving Ye 45 yuan per month without interruption. As they say, "husband and wife are like firewood and rice," and as firewood and rice were not lacking, there was rarely any dispute. Unexpectedly, last winter in October, Ye's eldest daughter went to Li's place to collect living expenses and was insulted by Li. She told her mother, which greatly angered Ye. A rift developed between the legal wife and the mistress. Recently, Ye hired a lawyer and filed a lawsuit in the First Special District Local Court against He Jingrong, demanding cohabitation. Yesterday morning, Judge Mo Runhua held a hearing. Ye testified that she was thirty-five years old and married He Jingrong at the age of eighteen. She had three children with him: a sixteen-year-old daughter, an eleven-year-old son, and an eight-year-old daughter. He's mistress, Li Qunfang, is twenty-six years old and they have been having an affair for eight years. He has not returned home since he had an affair. Although her living expenses have been paid monthly, his obligation to cohabitate has not been fulfilled for a long time. She now demands that the defendant separate from his concubine and return home to cohabitate with her. When questioned, He Jingrong also admitted to being thirty-five years old and acknowledged the fact that he had been cohabitating with Li Qunfang for eight years. However, he claimed that although he had an affair, he still often returned home and that the plaintiff's demand for cohabitation was not an issue. As for separating from Li, it was not his wish. After the lawyers on both sides debated, the court announced that it would rule on the 15th of this month.

Two Important Announcements from the Shanghai Municipal Council of the Public Concession 147

The Shanghai Municipal Council of the Public Concession has recently issued two important announcements:

(1) Announcement that taxpayers may appeal property tax assessments.

(2) Collection of firearms, ammunition, and swords, etc., stored by residents within the concession. The original text of the two announcements is recorded below:

Property Tax Assessment Appeals

Announcement: Any taxpayer who is dissatisfied with the rental value assessed for the purpose of collecting property taxes may, within thirty days of receiving the assessment notice from the Bureau, obtain an appeal form from the Revenue Department, complete it, and submit it to the Bureau. The Board of Directors will, after seeking the opinion of the Property Tax Assessment Appeal Committee, decide whether to approve or reject the appeal. If an appeal is not filed within the specified period or is rejected after being filed, the rental value assessed by the Bureau shall be valid. This announcement is hereby made for general information.

Collection of Civilian-Owned Firearms

Announcement: Any person within the Public Concession who possesses unused firearms, ammunition, or swords, etc., should immediately hand them over to any police station within the concession. The police station shall issue an official receipt upon receipt and will destroy the items free of charge. This announcement is hereby made for general information.

Rickshaw Committee Violates Regulations - Special Zone Owners Held General Meeting Yesterday Morning 150

Delegating Five Representatives to Negotiate with the Municipal Council - Stop Paying Membership Fees and Demand Reorganization of the Mutual Aid Society

The rickshaw guild of the Special Zone held an emergency meeting of owners at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday morning at 8:00 a.m. regarding the Mutual Aid Society's non-compliance with regulations, forced collection of mutual aid fees, and rickshaw samples, and issued a declaration. The details are recorded separately below.

Meeting Proposals: At 8:00 a.m. yesterday morning, the guild held a meeting in the auditorium of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. Gu Songmao, Wang Kunyi, Jin Chunlin, and others, totaling six hundred, attended. Gu Songmao, Hou Shaoan (Hou Wan'an representing), and Lu Dexin served as the presidium. Wang Yucheng from the Municipal Party Department and Li Ruzhang from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce attended to provide guidance. Gu Songmao first reported on the negotiations with the Municipal Council. After discussion (1) The Mutual Aid Society has exceeded the trial period, according to the regulations, the rickshaw owners and pullers should be responsible for the guild affairs, but the Rickshaw Committee refused to participate, how should it be dealt with? It was resolved to demand reorganization, and not pay the Mutual Aid Society fees from June onwards. (2) New rickshaw sample case, it was resolved to maintain the old style, with cleanliness and sturdiness as the principle. (3) The rickshaw registration incident case, it was resolved to cancel the registration restriction, in order to maintain the business of the rickshaw owners and the livelihood of the pullers. (4) Nomination of negotiation representatives, it was resolved to nominate Yin Zhiling, Hou Shaoan, Gu Songmao, Wang Kunyi, and Lu Desheng as representatives to negotiate with the Municipal Council.

Issued Declaration: The guild issued a declaration saying, "Our Special Zone's public rickshaw owners, since the Municipal Council established the Rickshaw Committee, proposed various suggestions for the new rickshaw industry system last spring. In addition to the first three items being put on hold, the rest, such as reducing the rent, changing the rickshaw samples, rickshaw owner licenses, rickshaw puller registration, etc., were not carefully reviewed, and the Rickshaw Affairs Committee was set up to specialize in its affairs. Not only were the above items implemented one by one, but also the Mutual Aid Society was set up, and the expenses required were the responsibility of the rickshaw owners to raise from the pullers, and ordered to pay in advance, regardless of damaging the rickshaw case and exploiting the pullers, and arbitrarily acted on their own. The representatives of the industry have repeatedly stated their grievances and requested improvements, which were ineffective, causing great indignation, so that both sides insisted, and the situation was very serious. On August 6th of the same year, the Municipal Council convened a meeting of the Rickshaw Committee and rickshaw merchants, and the result of the discussion was that all the agreed-upon methods, regarding the Mutual Aid Society, were resolved to try for eight months. Now that the trial period of the guild has expired, examining the past situation, all are showy and grandiose, in order to position private individuals and chat to decorate the facade, the money obtained by gathering sweat is all spent without名无买, and there is no indication of what the pullers urgently need. The representatives of the industry made reasonable and well-intentioned recommendations and repeatedly suggested to Chairman Mai of the guild to amend the constitution, in order to enhance the ability to do things and conform to the original intention of benefiting the society. Unexpectedly, the chairman stubbornly held his own opinions and did not adopt them. He was arrogant and did not allow others to participate in the deliberations. Although the representatives of the industry are members of the guild's board of directors, it seems that they are not allowed to consult any guild affairs at all. Thinking that the guild is called the rickshaw pullers' mutual aid, examining the name and studying the nature, the pullers and related rickshaw owners should be consulted and handled, and it is by no means that administrative personnel can manipulate it at will, but they actually concurrently assume the special power, forming a monopoly, and to this extent, how can its oppression be imagined? As for the new rickshaw sample, it needs to be agreed by the rickshaw merchants, with firmness, simplicity, and hygiene as the main points, and not focusing on flashy and other styles, which is recorded in the agreement of August 6th, and can be examined. However, the Rickshaw Committee first came up with its own unique ideas and manufactured rickshaw samples that were not suitable for public use, without giving the parties concerned sufficient consideration. More than 130 rickshaws that were pried were ordered to imitate and drive, although the rickshaw owners explained in detail how the new rickshaws were floating, not firm, and how heavy they were, the Rickshaw Committee turned a blind eye, and after feeling that it was not applicable, they did not think of thoroughly reforming it, and still followed the gourd, slightly changing it, and did not publicly discuss it with the rickshaw owners from beginning to end. Various measures show that the Rickshaw Committee violated the provisions of the equal agreement of August 6th last year. Our rickshaw owners are under this mandatory policy, and the business is declining day by day. The indignation is inevitable. The whole assembly is gathered to discuss the main points to deal with as follows: (1) The Mutual Aid Society is organized freely and independently by the paying pullers and responsible owners, and the members of the Rickshaw Committee must not concurrently hold the Mutual Aid Society affairs, so as to prevent despotism. (2) The amount of mutual aid should be discussed and determined by the pullers and the owners to determine an appropriate limit. (3) The new rickshaw sample must seek the consent of both the owner and the puller, and must not be determined by the Rickshaw Committee, so as to be suitable for public use. The above points are the legal struggle of our colleagues. We respectfully request all chambers of commerce, all colleagues, and all sectors of society to unite and help, and this is declared for your reference."

Safeguarding Business Safety of Merchants and Citizens

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce previously received a letter from the New Pharmaceutical Industry Association, stating that a Russian, Hutchinson, arbitrarily searched the Jihua Pharmacy, and asked the Public Concession Municipal Council to investigate. Then, it received a reply from the Municipal Council, stating that Hutchinson was not a staff member of the bureau. The letter said, "Respectfully, I have received your bureau's reply to the Jihua Hall Pharmacy matter of the 8th of this month. After checking this matter, according to what is said in your reply, then the Hutchinson is not a staff member of your bureau, and it is said that there was a similar case in the Hongkou Police Station in the past. It can be seen that Hutchinson is indeed a person who is not at peace. It can be seen that he went to the Jihua Hall Pharmacy this time and caused trouble under a false name, and there is a suspicion of trespassing into people's houses and attempted extortion. The police station in charge did not find out Hutchinson's nationality and charged him with the due guilt in the court in charge, which did not fulfill his duty to protect the business safety of merchants and citizens. The corresponding letter is sent to your bureau for inspection and handling, and I hope to see the reply."

Fire Behind the South Railway Station; One Person Burned to Death 156

Head Burned, Limbs Incomplete; Name Unknown, a Very Tragic Sight

In the Dachangxiang South Goods Store, a double-front store opened by Gong Wenxiang, a Chongming native, located at Nos. 252 and 254, the corner of the South Railway Station Road behind the South Railway Station of the local court on Yuannan Station Road, a fire broke out suddenly at 1:35 the night before. The fire was extinguished after the fire brigades from various districts drove to the scene. A total of three buildings were destroyed, and the fire also spread to one floor of the Wantai Tea Shop at No. 258. Yesterday afternoon, a male corpse was dug out of the rubble. Because the partners of Dachangxiang fled after the fire broke out, it is unknown who the body is. The local guarantor Gu Xueyuan reported to the local court and requested an autopsy. Subsequently, Prosecutor Lei Binzhang was commissioned to lead Inspector Xuan Zhiming to the scene. The autopsy revealed that the corpse's head was burned, and the limbs were incomplete. However, the scrotum was not completely burned, otherwise, it would be impossible to distinguish between male and female. The condition was extremely tragic, and it was determined that he was burned to death. The grid was filled and ordered to be placed in a coffin to await instructions.

Zhang Damin Sues Tang Jisan Case Rescheduled for Further Hearing at 2:00 PM on the 17th of This Month 160

The late famous movie star, Ruan Lingyu, a woman from Zhongshan, Guangdong, fell in love with Zhang Damin, who was from the same hometown, and they got together. Ruan then lived with Tang Jisan, who was also from the same hometown. The court summoned them according to the lawsuit. The first time, the court was ordered to reschedule because the defendants did not arrive. Later, on March 8th, the court reopened the trial. Unexpectedly, Ruan felt stimulated and committed suicide by swallowing a large amount of sleeping pills the day before. The rescue was ineffective, and she died. On the 8th, only the defendant Tang Jisan appeared in court with his defense lawyer Jiang Yiping. Because the plaintiff Zhang Damin did not arrive, it was postponed. The occurrence of this case attracted the attention of movie fans all over Shanghai and caused a sensation. Ruan's suicide was reported in newspapers. Later, someone even rumored that Ruan was not dead and had escaped back to her hometown of Zhongshan County and was arrested. Zhang Damin rushed to hear the news and waited for various rumors. In the end, the case was delayed until now, and the news has been silent for two months. Now it is learned that Zhang's case against Ruan and Tang has been scheduled by Judge Zhang Chaozuo of the Second Special Court to reopen the trial at 2:00 PM on the 17th of this month. Summons have been issued and dispatched by the court police to both parties yesterday, and both lawyers have been notified. It is expected that there will be a fierce debate between the two parties at that time.

Summary of Bank Inspection Reports 172

The 121st Inspection Report on the Issuance Reserve of the Central Bank stated, "In accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank Ordinance, this association is responsible for inspecting the issuance exchange reserve of this bank. The 121st inspection was held in the Issuance Bureau of this bank on May 10th, 1935. The results of the inspection are announced as follows: (A) The total amount of exchange coupons issued is 91,535,351 yuan, including 84,637,573 yuan for banknotes and 6,897,778 yuan for subsidiary currency coupons. The total amount of exchange coupon reserve is 91,535,351 yuan, including 71,128,351 yuan for cash reserve. The cash reserve includes 68,418,610 yuan stored in the issuance vault of this bank, 1,041,754 yuan stored in branch banks in various ports, and 1,824,987 yuan stored in fellow banks. The guarantee reserve is 19,200,000 yuan converted into silver dollars. (B) The total amount of customs gold exchange coupons issued is 373,324.70 yuan. The total amount of customs gold exchange coupon reserve is 373,324.70 yuan. The reserve includes 7,251.95 taels of standard gold, which is 373,324.70 yuan in customs gold at the fixed price of 50779. According to Article 1 of the Central Bank Exchange Coupon Regulations, the cash reserve is 60% and the guarantee reserve is 40%. The result of this inspection is that the cash exceeds 60% and the guarantee is less than 40%, which is in accordance with the regulations. This is hereby reported. May 11, 1935, Li Fusun, Chairman of the Supervisory Board of the Central Bank, Supervisors Xie Mingdong, Bei Songsun, Qin Runxiang, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Shanhou, and Ji Qing."

The Issuance Reserve Inspection Report of the China Industrial Bank stated, "The issuance vault and the operating vault of the China Industrial Bank have always been completely separated. According to the regulations of the bank's charter, the cash reserve is above 70% and the guarantee reserve is above 30%. On the 10th of this month, the accountant Wang Zikang and the directors and supervisors Xu Jiqing and Xu Busun checked the results as follows: The total amount of exchange coupons issued is 6,440,000 yuan. The total amount of exchange coupon reserve is 6,440,000 yuan. The cash reserve is 4,910,000 yuan. The guarantee reserve is 1,520,000 yuan. The above two items, the cash reserve accounts for 76% and the guarantee reserve accounts for 24%. This is hereby reported. 24.5.11."

The Honor of Qu Zhibu Hospital 173

Qu Daofu Hospital on Penglai Road and the branch on Zhonghua Road, Xiaodongmen, were founded by Dr. Qu Zhibu. The facilities are complete, and the medical affairs are devoted to the poor and sick, and they can especially empathize. Sometimes, medicine and industry are combined, so no one in the south and the concession does not know about Qu Daofu Hospital. A few days ago, Shi Wuxi suffered from lower leg ulcers on his lower limbs, which had not healed for many years, but there was no pain. Unexpectedly, starting last month, it suddenly became red and swollen and gradually intensified, causing him to be mentally confused. The family felt terrified and, through the introduction of relatives and friends, sent him to Qu Daofu Hospital on Penglai Road, Nanshi, for treatment. When he arrived at the hospital, he was dying, and doctors Yan Qingkang and Zhu Qi diagnosed that it was erysipelas, which would soon lead to septicemia. He was old and weak, and his heart was easily weakened. He was in critical condition and his life was hanging by a thread. He was hospitalized for treatment. After the two doctors carefully diagnosed and treated him, they administered various serums and other emergency treatments, and also transfused blood for him. After a week, he gradually turned from danger to safety, and he was completely healthy after a month. The family and relatives were grateful for the kindness of re-creation, so they made a plaque to praise the magical skills of the two doctors. The inscription reads "Turning Hands into Miracles," with the note: "My mother suffered from left leg ulcers for several months. At the end of last year, due to her old age, she could not support herself and her illness worsened day by day. Doctors Yan and Zhu diagnosed that it was erysipelas, and with their efforts to save her, she turned from danger to safety. The merit is comparable to re-creation. January 1935, Shi Wuxi Yi." The plaque was sent by the patient's family to Qu Daofu Hospital yesterday.

Starting from the third issue, it has been entirely in classical Chinese. This issue includes a brief history of the members of the Guanhua Harmonica Quintet, an article on the Suzhou Harmonica World, a detailed program of the Grand Wu Concert, the sheet music for the Wedding March played at the concert, and practical harmonica repair methods, etc. This morning, the magazine specially dispatched commissioners to rush to Suzhou to distribute 1,000 copies at the Grand Wu Music Conference. All Shanghai newspaper vendors and the Shanghai Magazine Company have it for sale. Overseas readers can subscribe for the whole year for one yuan, including postage. Subscriptions with postage of one cent can be sent to the Promotion Department of the magazine on the second floor of Guiming Spectacles Shop at the Old North Gate.

"Guoxun" Ten-Day Magazine - "Guoxun" Ten-Day Magazine has been published for nearly half a year and has been widely circulated. The total number has exceeded 20,000 copies, making it one of the most widely sold new publications at home and abroad. The writers include Jiang Wenyu, Chen Binhe, Xiang Yuancun, Huang Yanpei, Yang Shuyu, Ren Jinpin, Zhang Xucheng, etc. There are also many specially invited experts, so the content is extremely rich, and the price is low. The whole year of thirty-four issues is one yuan domestically and two yuan overseas, including postage. All post offices across the country can subscribe. The general distribution is located at No. 80 Hualong Road, Shanghai.

"Sunday Guide" Issue No. 3 - The third issue of "Sunday Guide" from the "Sunday Guide" office at No. 363 Foch Road, Shanghai, has been published today. Key contents include "Towards the World of War Scars," "An Analysis of Hitler's Re-armament," "Abyssinia and the Relationship between Italy, France, and England," "Two Routes of Today's World Economy," "British Foreign Policy," "Full Text of the Franco-Soviet Mutual Assistance Treaty," and "Stalin in the Eyes of Two Great Anglo-French Thinkers I (Wells and Barbusse)." The cover is printed in two colors with "The Road to War." The price is five cents per issue. During the special price period, direct subscriptions to the magazine are one yuan per year or one yuan and one cent for half a year. The general sales agent is the Shanghai Magazine Company.

Calligraphy and Painting News 177

Opening of the Liuyingtang Calligraphy and Painting Exhibition - The owner of Liuyingtang is a famous collector from eastern Zhejiang. This time, he has exhibited more than 1,000 pieces of calligraphy and painting by famous artists collected throughout his life, displayed at the Lakes Society on Guizhou Road, Beijing Road. The exhibition is open to the public starting yesterday. Such as Dong Qichang, Zhou Dongcun, Sun Kehong, and Wen Zhengming of the Ming Dynasty, and Xiang Kongzhang, Wang Luhao, and Ren Bonian of the Qing Dynasty, all are genuine masterpieces. Especially the works of Ren Bonian are the most numerous, about forty pieces, lined up on the walls, which are very beautiful. It is a great opportunity to satisfy the eyes of the Shanghai people.

Weather Report 179

The meteorological forecast from the Xujiahui Observatory at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that there are cyclones and rain in the vicinity of Shandong and the Yellow Sea due to the passage of a small low pressure system moving eastward. The middle and lower reaches of the Yangtze River are mostly clear and hot, gradually cloudy. The wind is from the northwest to the north. The East Sea and the Taiwan Strait are cloudy and foggy. The wind is from the southeast to the southwest. Also, before 2:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in the city in the past fourteen hours was 91.5 degrees, and the lowest was 67.1 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 76.6 degrees, and the lowest was 50.0 degrees.

Letter to the Editor 180

To the editor, I have read the article in your May 11th newspaper about the two female students from Zhengfeng Middle School who attempted suicide due to failing their exams, and there are some inaccuracies. The report stated that Wang Dingyi was the first defendant, but I am definitely not the first defendant. The claims that Huang Yangzhen approached the family of the first defendant Wang Dingyi and that Wang Dingyi colluded with Zhu Zheyun to frame Chen Pinqing, and that they arranged for Chen Pinqing to be sent to the port, and that the next day they arranged for Chen Pinqing to go to Wusong, etc., are all misunderstandings. Because I and the plaintiff Ms. Chen Pinqing are colleagues, but we do not communicate, so I am writing to request your newspaper to quickly correct the record. Respectfully, Wang Dingyi, May 11th.

Sports News

CU Wins Both JNU Track and Field Championships - 400m Ties National Record - Dong Shu-Zhao's Triumphant Performance at 51.4 Seconds - Six JNU Records Broken Including 100m 181

Group Events to be Piloted Next Year

Nanjing, 11th - The JNU track and field meet continued this afternoon at CU. The results of the finals saw six JNU records broken, including the 100m, 800m, high hurdles, low hurdles, shot put, and high jump. Dong Shu-Zhao's 400m tied the national record, greatly enhancing the event. The Central University team is well-equipped with talent and has worked hard to win both track and field championships, which is no accident. The closing ceremony was held at 5:30 PM, with Chairman Rong Qizhao presenting awards. CU President Luo delivered a speech hoping that the spirit and achievements of this meeting would be shared with national and world competitions to promote the spirit of our nation. In the evening, the CU Sports Department hosted a banquet for all referees, which ended at 10:00 PM.

400 Meters - Looking at the results of each event, although no new national records were discovered, most of them were excellent. Dong Shu-Zhao, the middle-distance star of Guanghua University, won two first-place finishes and the individual championship. His 400m time of 52.4 seconds equaled the national record set by Liu Changchun at the North China Games in 1929. This achievement has finally been rediscovered after six years. With Dong's talent and hard work, it will not be difficult to tighten it up further and break the record in the future, which is also what we hope for from Dong. His 800m time of 2 minutes and 6 seconds also set a new meet record, which is commendable.

Meet Records - In addition to Dong Shu-Zhao's 400m tying the national record, there were also six new meet records set. Liu Yingjun of Central University at 11.6 seconds was the most outstanding, only 0.4 seconds away from the national record. His long jump of 6.55 meters was also respectable. Huang Feilong of Jinan University, who was unsuccessful in the preliminary selections for the Shanghai International Games, set a new meet record of 11.2 seconds in the sprint, which is rare. He was also satisfied with his 200m at 23.6 seconds.

Total Scores of Each School - The scores of each school in the track and field meet are as follows: "Track" (1) CU 36 points, (2) Guanghua 23 points, (3) Fudan 12 points, (4) Medical South 10 points, (5) Chizhi 5 points, (6) Jinling 1 point; "Field" (1) CU 48 points, (2) Fudan 17 points, (3) Jinan 8 points, (4) Jinling 4 points.

Annual Meeting Held Yesterday - The annual meeting of the JNU Athletic Association was held at the CU gymnasium yesterday morning. Yu Jie of Jinan, Wu Yunrui and Wu Zheng of CU, Shen Kunnan and Wu Shijie of Fudan, Wang Fudan of Chizhi, Xu Shaowu of Jinling, and Peng Wenyu of Guanghua attended. Chaired by Rong Qizhao, the meeting resolved: (1) Regarding the athletic qualifications in the constitution, add the annotation "These ten credits are required for the athlete to graduate" under the original eleven credits. (2) The sports events to be held next semester are basketball, volleyball, and track and field in the fall. (Because the all-around event is related to the National Games, it will be temporarily incorporated into the National Games.) (3) Pilot group events. The 100m and 12-pound shot put will be held next semester, with all first-year university students participating. Please specify the detailed rules, Mr. Wu Zheng. (4) The next semester's tennis championship will be held at Guanghua, and Peng Wenyu will be responsible for planning. The order of assignment of other standing committee members must be notified one month in advance. (5) Re-elect the next term of officers: President Rong Qizhao, Vice President Wang Fudan, Treasurer Yu Jie, Secretary Peng Wenyu.

International Sports Chinese Supplementary Selection: Wang Jihuai and Others Selected 187

Five Supplementary Candidates All Admitted

Because Luo Hu, Wang Jihuai, Zhang Jiakui, Fu Baolu, and Chen Jiayou of the Shanghai Chinese Athletic Games Committee had previously achieved good results, but were unable to participate in the preliminary competition due to certain reasons, a trial competition was specially held yesterday afternoon in Shen Garden. All five of the above-mentioned individuals arrived on time and demonstrated their respective skills. Because there was no competition, the results were mediocre. After discussion by the committee, it was deemed that they were all qualified and were admitted to serve as representatives to this International Games. The results of the five individuals are listed below:

Luo Qian: Discus: 33.59 meters

Zhang Jiakui: Triple Jump: 13.46 meters

Wang Jihuai: Long Jump: 6.39 meters

Fu Baolu: Pole Vault: 3.55 meters

Chen Jiayou: High Hurdles: 18 seconds

Baofu and Wang He Perform Pole Vault Together

Yesterday, only Fu Baolu was scheduled for a formal pole vault demonstration. Temporarily, Wang He, who had achieved excellent results in long jump, triple jump, pole vault, and high jump in the previous day's preliminary competition, accompanied him to enhance the interest. They started jumping from 3 meters, gradually increasing to 3.55 meters. Wang He cleared it on his third attempt, while Baolu cleared it on his fourth attempt. When the height was increased to 3.60 meters, both Wang and Fu were unable to clear it due to fatigue.

Zhang Jiakui's Triple Jump, Wang Jihuai's Jumping Speed

Zhang Jiakui's first triple jump already achieved a result of 12.46 meters. The second jump regressed to 13.29 meters. Ultimately, due to running and jumping alone, without any rest time or competitive interest, he stopped after three jumps. Wang Jihuai was too cautious in the long jump, and his foot did not reach the board when he took off, which significantly affected his performance. He repeatedly stepped in half a foot for more than ten attempts, which was a great pity. His stride was naturally difficult to be accurate. As a result, he recorded a distance of 6.39 meters. Wang He also accompanied him in jumping yesterday, although there was no official record, judging from the distance, it was also not bad.

Chen Jiayou's High Hurdles and Luo Qian's Discus

Chen Jiayou suffered a left leg cramp yesterday. He almost stumbled before the start. His result in the 100-meter dash was mediocre. Later, he gave up the 200-meter dash and ran the 110-meter high hurdles. He started alone, but the result was 18 seconds. His speed and stride at the start were excellent. Unfortunately, he brushed against the fourth hurdle, knocking it down. After this setback, the accuracy of his stride was affected, and he also unfortunately knocked down the ninth hurdle. Otherwise, his result could have improved. Luo Qian's discus result of 33.59 meters was not as good as Weng Gongwan's 33.738 meters in the preliminary competition.

Eighth District Elementary School Joint Sports Meet: Pengpu Wins the Overall Championship 188

More Than 200 Athletes from 13 Participating Schools; Rural Elementary Schools Participating in Joint Sports Meet for the First Time

The Nanshi District Elementary School Joint Sports Meet held its first day yesterday in the Eighth District. The venue was the Jinnan University sports ground. More than 300 athletes from 13 participating schools, in addition to 16 sections of group exercises. Details are recorded as follows:

Enthusiastic Participation

Schools in the Zhenru and Pengpu districts have all participated, including Zhangcun, Zhenru, Shiyan, Jinxiang, Pengpu, Yanlong, Guanlong, Xuyuan, Ganlu, Meicun, Pengcheng, Changtou, Gucun, and other 13 schools. Among them, except for Zhenru Elementary School, the other 12 schools have never participated in the city's elementary school joint sports meet. This year, due to district events, travel is convenient, so they can participate enthusiastically. Chief referee Yu Hengzhi was absent; Sun Yiguang substituted in the morning, and Wang Keyong substituted in the afternoon. The East Asia Institute of Physical Education specially dispatched six students to the venue to serve as referees.

Commendable Spirit

Yesterday at 9 a.m., students from various schools had already arrived. The opening ceremony was held first. Chairman Shi Deheng gave a report, followed by a speech by He Jiefu, a representative of the Eleventh District Education Association. The sports meet then began. Although the track and field results were unremarkable, the athletes were all children from rural areas, and their hardworking spirit was particularly commendable. Most of the elementary school students in rural areas could not afford school uniforms, so although the clothing was not uniform during the group exercises, it further demonstrated their spirit of struggle. Yesterday, because the scales were inaccurate, the winning athletes in the male and female B and C groups still needed to be reweighed separately. Prizes were awarded at another time because the time was insufficient.

Minor Dispute

Yesterday, the order at the venue was maintained by the Shiyan Elementary School Boy Scouts, who were quite dedicated. Later, a dispute arose over the rankings of the boys' B group high jump results with the physical education teacher of Shiyan Elementary School. They questioned the referee, and a misunderstanding occurred between the two sides. For a time, all the Boy Scouts abandoned their duties and gathered around the command platform, surrounding it. Unscrupulous individuals also took the opportunity to engage in extra actions. Fortunately, Chen Kemei, the director of Dada Shizhong, stopped them on the spot, preventing a major disaster. However, the school's faculty should be held responsible for this bad phenomenon. Regardless of whether the referee's records were in error, students should not take direct action. Furthermore, these elementary school students should not be allowed to develop the bad habit of not abiding by sportsmanship. The total scores of each school are as follows:

Education News

Ten Professors Issue a General Response Explaining the Meaning of Chinese-Based Culture 192

Recognize That the Need at This Time and Place is to Fight for National Survival; Anti-Imperialism and Anti-Feudalism are Inevitable Missions in the Construction Process; Express Determination to Reject Restoration and Complete Westernization

Since the professors issued the "Declaration of Chinese-Based Cultural Construction," it has had an impact on the whole country in a few months. However, there have been many misunderstandings and doubts. The professors recently issued a general response, which is recorded below. On January 10th of this year, we issued a "Declaration of Chinese-Based Cultural Construction," and at the same time, we held research-oriented symposiums, produced consultation forms, collected important documents, and publicly solicited papers, hoping to obtain a concise and comprehensive guiding principle for cultural construction from these aspects. Now, because the academic community has embraced this idea with great enthusiasm and contributed many valuable opinions, and raised many noteworthy questions, especially regarding: 1. What is Chinese-based? 2. What is not being conservative? 3. What is not blindly following? 4. How is Chinese-based different from "Chinese learning as the foundation, Western learning for application"? 5. What are the needs of China at this time and place? 6. What is the attitude towards anti-imperialism and anti-feudalism? We believe it is necessary to respond. In the declaration, we reviewed the reasons for the shaking of Chinese culture after the eastward spread of Westernization by examining the historical development of Chinese culture, pointed out the problems of past failed movements, and advocated that future cultural construction should be based on China, and asserted that the needs of China at this time and place are the foundation of the Chinese-based culture. This clearly indicates that the Chinese-based culture we advocate is not a conservative inheritance, not a blind imitation, not a combination of Chinese essence and Western application, but a creation based on the needs and preparations of the entire nation at this time and place. We firmly believe that different times and places will not have exactly the same needs. The needs of China in the closed-door era and China after the opening of the door are completely different. The world powers in the position of aggressors and China in the position of being invaded also have their different needs. If we admit that each time and place has its own needs, then we should affirm that China at this time and place has its own special needs. The culture produced in response to this special need is of course different from the Chinese culture in the closed-door era or the culture of the world powers. The Chinese-based cultural construction we advocate should be based on this special need. Our belief is such, so the Chinese-based cultural construction we advocate does not promote restoration in the vertical direction, opposes complete Westernization in the horizontal direction, attaches importance to the problems of this time in time, and attaches importance to the environment of this place in space. We earnestly hope that our cultural construction can be consistent with the needs of this time and place.

Furthermore, since culture and the needs of time and place should be consistent, the form of culture should change and progress with the needs of time and place. Attempts to restore the old are not only conservative but simply courting death. If we believe that modern Chinese people should not live in the feudal era, then we should not hold a conservative attitude to prevent the evolution of culture. We must also support the trend of the times and strive to embark on a new and ever-changing future. Only in this way, one of our cultural construction guidelines should be not to be conservative. We adopt a rejection attitude towards any attempt to restore the old. We dare to say that the remnants of feudalism have no realistic value to be obsessed with. Any act of re-enacting history and reviving feudalism will inevitably fail. Even if there is accidental success, it is only a fleeting epiphyllum, a flashing bubble. Instead of creating artificial darkness and prolonging their own evolutionary process, people should go straight to the bright future and accelerate upward development.

For the needs of this time and place, we oppose conservatism. For the needs of this time and place, we also oppose blind adherence. We know that if culture is not combined with the needs of the times, it will lead to historical errors. If culture does not adapt to the conditions of the region, it will also lead to regional conflicts. Modern Chinese people should neither be obsessed with the remnants of the past nor worship idols from foreign lands. If foreign cultures are sufficient to nourish us, we should absorb them as much as possible, but we must make a careful selection based on the needs of this time and place. If we disregard the conditions of time and place and rashly advocate complete Westernization, it is not only turning the guest into the host but truly destroying oneself. Moreover, Western culture itself is not a unified entity. Is not the conflict between capitalist culture and socialist culture a contradiction in Western culture itself? What exactly is meant by "completely accepting"? Is it to completely accept capitalist culture, to completely accept socialist culture, or to completely accept both capitalist and socialist cultures? If it is believed that there is a common foundation or nature between capitalist and socialist cultures that can be completely accepted, it is not known that each culture has its unique system. Since capitalist culture and socialist culture are built on different social relations, any part of their systems cannot be the same. May I ask the proponents of complete Westernization, where do you start Westernizing from? We not only oppose conservatism and blind adherence, but also reject the so-called "Chinese essence, Western application" proposition. Proponents of "Chinese essence, Western application" believe that Western material civilization has its valuable aspects, and Chinese spiritual civilization also has its valuable aspects. If Western material civilization is governed by Chinese spiritual civilization, that would be the most ideal combination. Those who hold this view mostly believe that there is an insurmountable iron limit between material and spirit. Material progress and spiritual progress are completely unrelated. Western material civilization has no soul, and Chinese spiritual civilization has no body. Therefore, it should combine Chinese spiritual civilization with Western material civilization to form a unified whole. But in fact, this is not the case. Material and spirit are two aspects of the same thing and cannot be separated at all. We cannot say that China only has spiritual civilization, nor can we say that the West only has material civilization. When it comes to essence and application, whatever essence there is, there will be application. Whatever application there is, there must be essence. Talking about Chinese essence and Western application simply does not make sense. The Chinese-based cultural construction should be based on the needs of this time and place, needless to say. What exactly are the needs of China at this time and place? First, the people's lives need to be enriched. The lives of the Chinese people are very poor. Not to mention that in terms of material things, it is inferior to others. The lack of knowledge, the disorder of actions, the decline of will, and the dryness of emotions are also symbols of the bankruptcy of the people's lives. Secondly, the people's livelihood needs to be developed. Foreign trade and industrial conditions are the measures of the people's livelihood. China is now a country with trade deficits, backward industries, and a collapsed countryside. How can we not strive for the development of the people's livelihood? Finally, the survival of the nation needs to be guaranteed. Since the Opium War, the forces of imperialism have continued to invade, from cities to villages, densely laying the network of imperialism that binds the freedom of the Chinese nation. The Chinese territory nibbled away and swallowed by whales has only been shrinking day by day. The Chinese sovereignty seized by trickery and force has long been painfully stripped away. In addition to economic exploitation without any end, the blood of the entire Chinese nation is about to dry up. This is also a matter of life and death at the moment. To sum up, the needs of China at this time and place are: "To enrich the lives of the people, develop the livelihood of the nation, and strive for the survival of the nation." Therefore, Chinese-based cultural construction is a manifestation of national self-confidence and a positive creation. Anti-imperialism and anti-feudalism are inevitable missions in this creative process. Wang Xinming, He Bingsong, Wu Yugan, Sun Hanbing, Huang Wenshan, Tao Xisheng, Zhang Yi, Chen Gaoyong, Fan Zhongyun, Sa Mengwu.

Spring and Autumn Children's Weekly

Mother's Day 195

By Zhen

Little friends, what holiday is today? I think very few know. You should know that today is Mother's Day.

Where did we come from? We came from our mother's womb. Our mother suffered for more than ten months to bring us into the world. From then on, our mother was even more hardworking, always paying attention to us. She is always thinking about us all day long.

Clothing: When spring arrives, your mother is busy making thin clothes for you. When winter arrives, she is busy making cotton clothes for you again. And you don't think about it at all. Where did your clothes come from? They are all the crystallization of your mother's thousands of stitches. You wear them, but you are still not satisfied, thinking this is too big, that is too small. Should it be like this?

Food: Your mother always chooses good things for you to eat, and also tells you not to eat fatty meat, and that fish is too fishy. What about herself? She eats what you leave behind. What do you think when you see this?

In addition, the bed you sleep on at night is modern, with a spring mattress. In winter, it is a silk cotton quilt and a hot water bottle. In summer, it is a Wenzhou mat and a gauze mosquito net. How deep is your mother's love for you!

Mother loves us so much. How should we repay her? Is it some superficial ceremony? No, definitely not. Our responsibility now is to study hard. That is the only way to repay her.

The Story of Han Xin 196

By Tu Hongxia

Marquis Han Xin of Huaiyin was a meritorious official who helped Emperor Gaozu of Han, Liu Bang. Before he became successful, he was an extremely poor and helpless young man. Even now, there are still two historical sites in Huai'an:

(1) Crotch Bridge: In the southwest corner of Huai'an City, there is a place called Crotch Bridge. At that time, Han Xin was still poor and humble. He often went out with a sword hanging from his waist. One day, while passing through the area, many rogue youths said to him: "Han Xin! You often come out with a sword. If you have the ability, show it and compete with us. Otherwise, you can only walk under our crotches!" Han Xin smiled, lowered his head, and walked under their crotches. The rogues all laughed loudly.

(2) Fishing Terrace: When Han Xin was poor, he had no way to make a living, so he fished by the small pond two miles outside the west gate of Huai'an. However, he could not catch any fish every day. Fortunately, there was a washerwoman who often gave him food, allowing him to get through the difficult and difficult times, and achieve great success. Therefore, after Han Xin became a high-ranking official, he once gave a thousand gold to thank the washerwoman, but the washerwoman firmly refused to accept it. To this day, there is still a washerwoman temple and a washerwoman tomb in the vicinity of Huai'an, so that later generations can admire her!

Today's Questions 197

— Zhu Ying

Little friends, today is Sunday again. What are you all doing hiding at home today?

Did you get up as early today as you usually do on weekdays? If you got up late, then you should ask yourselves: "What is the healthy way to get up, early or late?"

After breakfast, did you open your schoolbags and review the books you studied during the week? Should you review on Sundays? Or should you not touch books and just have fun, because Sunday is a day of rest?

Younger siblings naturally love to fool around with you, argue with you, and fight with you on Sundays. Classmates will naturally come to tease you to play football, billiards, or invite you out for a walk or hike on Sundays. Neighbor children will naturally come to drag you to play "bandit mountain", act out "The Iron Rooster", or roll copper coins and play cigarette cards on Sundays. Among these kinds of games, which one do you plan to choose today?

This afternoon, if your mother is playing mahjong, then how do you plan to pass the time? If your mother is afraid you will make noise and gives you money, then do you plan to go to the "one copper coin for the top prize" stall at the entrance of the lane to gamble for candy? Or put it in your savings box?

The above questions are all today's questions, and they are all very easy to answer. Little friends, try to answer them.

Things You Must Know 199

— Mu Liang

After a piece of "Things You Must Know" was published in this journal in previous issues, here are a few more things you must know to tell you, little friends:

The flag of Denmark was created in 1290 and is the oldest national flag in the world.

The largest flower in the world grows on the island of Sumatra and is shaped like a wheel.

The streets of London, the capital of England, are 2,600 miles long and have a population of over 5 million.

The capital of Spain is the highest city in Europe, built on a mountain peak more than 2,200 feet above sea level.

There are more than 270,000 large factories in the United States.

The Nile River in Africa is the river with the most fish in the world.

The Canadian railway runs across the American continent and is more than 3,000 miles long; before the Russian Siberian Railway was completed, this road was the longest line in the world.

The speed at which whales swim is between ten and twenty miles per hour.

Light can travel around the Earth eight times in one second.

Mr. Science Performs Magic 200

— He Gongchao

Lifting a cup of water with a string

Mr. Science is back on stage. In his right hand he holds a glass, which is full of water. In his left hand he holds a circular piece of cardboard—slightly larger than the mouth of the glass—and a string. He says to the children on the stage:

"Little friends, we usually get water with a bucket or a basin; today we won't use these two things; we will just use this string and this piece of cardboard to lift this cup of water. Among you, who can do it?"

There was not a single answering voice from the audience, everyone felt that this was impossible to do.

"In fact, as long as you understand a little scientific common sense, this thing is very easy to do. Now, watch me do it."

He first punched a small hole in the center of the cardboard, then threaded the string through the hole: he also took out a candle stub from his pocket, struck a match, lit it, and poured the candle oil on the string, so that it would stick to the cardboard and not fall off.

After doing this, he covered the mouth of the glass with the cardboard, using his fingers to tighten the surroundings so that there was no gap for air to get in. At this time, you see him slowly straighten the string, slowly lift it up, haha! This cup full of water, which is quite heavy, is suspended in the air, very firm, very stable, and not a single drop of water spills out.

So the children in the audience were all stunned in surprise.

"Little friends, do you know why this cup doesn't fall down? It turns out that there is a lot of air pressure on our top, bottom, left, right, front, and back. This air pressure is called atmospheric pressure.

"Now this cup is full of water, there is no air inside, and the cardboard is tightly covering the top, so that the air outside the cup cannot get in. Therefore, only the air above the cardboard is pressing down, so that the cardboard is firmly attached to the mouth of the cup and cannot fall off; at the same time, the air below the cup is also pressing upwards, holding the cup up. In this way, the cup is suspended in the air by the string and will not fall down.

"Now turn the cup upside down, will this cardboard fall off?—No, you see, for the same reason, it will not fall off either."

You Can Seek Fish by Climbing a Tree 201

— Yi De

Little friends! You must be surprised when you see this title. "Seeking fish by climbing a tree" is an idiom, a metaphor for something impossible to obtain. Because fish are in the water, how can you get them by climbing a tree? But I want to tell you: "You can seek fish by climbing a tree."

There is a kind of fish called the "climbing perch", which is produced in the fresh water of India, Malaysia, and other places. Its fins are particularly hard. When it lives in the water day and night and feels a little unhappy, it wants to go to the shore to play. When it comes from the water to the shore, it uses the spines of its pelvic and abdominal fins to support itself on the ground, and uses its pectoral fins to crawl, just like a beast walking on its feet. Although it doesn't walk as lightly as a beast, it can walk up from the beach, step by step, climb the reeds on the shore, and walk all the way to the reeds on the shore. In the water, it breathes with gills like other fish, but when it reaches the shore, it also has a substitute for gills that can breathe air and does not feel difficult; this is also one of the reasons why it can safely go ashore.

According to general speculation, its hard fins can be used as feet to walk and climb reeds, and if there are big trees by the river, it would certainly be possible for it to climb the big trees. Perhaps it is because there are no big trees by the river, but no one has ever seen it climb a big tree. Otherwise, the idiom "seeking fish by climbing a tree" would become a real saying.

Turtle and Duck 204

— Yan Xinquan

Little friends! Now I will tell you an interesting arithmetic problem. When you are free, you may as well ask your brothers, sisters, or friends to see if they can figure it out.

"A basket of turtles and a load of ducks, there are only forty-nine heads, and there are one hundred feet, how many turtles and how many ducks?"

But you have to explain to him: turtles have four feet and ducks only have two feet! After saying this, wait for him to calculate; if he really can't figure it out, then tell him the answer.

Answer: One turtle, forty-eight ducks.

Animal Small Talk 205

— Bing Yu

The lion has been known as the king of beasts since ancient times. Its shape is similar to that of a long-haired lion dog. The structure of its body is best suited for preying on other beasts. Its teeth have three kinds: incisors, canines, and molars. The canines and molars are very sharp. No matter what goes into its mouth, it will bite it into pieces. Its feet are the same as those of a cat, and its sense of touch is very sensitive. The shapes of male and female lions are very different. Male lions have silkworm hair and a majestic appearance. The hair is yellow-brown and produced in the sand dunes of East Africa and Southwest Asia, so the color of its hair is similar to the color of the sand dunes. Generally speaking, animals have a kind of protective coloration. The tiger and leopard have yellow ground and black patterns, which are similar to the grass leaves of the forest. The white fox and white bear are pure white, which is similar to the color of the snowy ice field. This is the natural advantage given to them to defend against enemies and obtain food. When lion cubs are first born, they are the same as cats and dogs. They will open their eyes after three days, and their bodies will have black spots. There are black stripes on their backs, which look like tigers and leopards. After growing up, the black stripes and spots gradually disappear. After being born, the lion cubs eat milk for two months, and then they will eat meat. After half a year, they will follow the mother lion to hunt beasts outside. The method of attacking other beasts is often to jump fiercely onto the beast's body and bite its neck to kill it. After eating, it must drink water. Every morning and evening, it drinks a large amount of water once. If it cannot eat all of the beast it has bitten to death at one time, it will carry it to a suitable place and cover the remains with wood leaves and dead grass to prevent them from being seen by other beasts, so that it can come and eat them next time. It hides in its lair during the day, and when the sun sets, it comes out to move around. Its bark is very loud, and all the beasts tremble when they hear its voice. It often accompanies a group of five or six lions and climbs onto the rocks in the sand dunes to roar loudly. When it roars, the earth shakes and the heavens move, and when the beasts hear its roar, they think that the lion is coming to harm them, and they all run east and west to escape. If we encounter a lion on the road, don't worry, because the lion will not bite us casually. If it is walking around looking east and west, then it must be going to the place of its companions. But when it is hungry, or when it is a female lion following lion cubs, then there is a danger to life. In Uganda, East Africa, when the railway was being built, the workers were often harmed by lions. A Colonel Paitaisong brought three thousand workers from India to live along the route by setting up tents. Unexpectedly, there were two lions nearby who smelled the scent of humans and came to the tents every night to harm people, so many workers were harmed by them. Although they tried all kinds of methods to capture it, the two lions were very bold. Every day when the sun went down, they would roar loudly, and in an instant they would run to the side of the tent, trying to eat people. The workers could not sleep peacefully every night, and took turns guarding outside the tents. Later, after they were killed one by one with machine guns, they were able to be safe and sound.

Story Picture - Thanks to the Donkey (Continued) 206

— Zhang Youjian

(1) After the cook kicked Fei'er into the sea, he quickly released a lifeboat to rescue Fei'er.

(2) While walking on the road, Fei'er and Rong'er both felt hungry. They saw a pot of hot wheat flour cakes placed on the window of a house, so the two of them took it and ate it.

(3) They were seen by the owner, and the two of them desperately ran away.

(4) Fei'er ate too much, and after running for a while, his stomach suddenly hurt, and he couldn't run anymore. Someone was chasing after them, and the two of them were very anxious.

(5) Rong'er suddenly saw a donkey eating grass, so he helped Fei'er to ride on it first, and then he rode on it himself.

(6) Unexpectedly, the donkey got angry when it saw strangers, kicked Fei'er down, and then came to bite Rong'er.

(7) The two of them fell so hard that their muscles and bones were sore, and they couldn't get up from the ground.

(8) Just then, an ambulance passed by and quickly carried the two of them into the car. At this time, Fei'er laughed and said to Rong'er: "Looking at it this way, it's thanks to this donkey; otherwise, how could we have returned home so quickly?"

The Adventures of Sinbad the Sailor (17) 207

— Xin Qing

I rested for a while, then got up to take a walk and see the place. I saw that all around were ripe fruits, and clear and clean streams flowed down the slopes, so I got food and drink. When night came, I lay down, but I couldn't sleep because I was afraid, and after dawn, I was very happy.

So I went out for a walk, but I didn't go far before I saw an old man on the bank of the stream. At first, I thought he was from a shipwreck, and he seemed weak and sick. I spoke to him, but he didn't answer me. He gestured to me to carry him on my back and walk across the stream together.

I thought he needed my help, so I helped him. When we reached the other side of the stream, I bent down so that he could get off easily.

However, this old man, whom I thought was very weak, did not get off my back. He raised his legs and wrapped them around my neck, and squeezed my throat so tightly that I thought I was going to suffocate. Finally, I fell down and fainted, but the old man was still holding on to me. When I regained my breath, he kicked me to make me stand up.

I reluctantly carried him closer to the trees, and he kept telling me to stop and find fruit to eat. He never left me all day, and when I lay down to sleep at night, he still clung to my neck. This went on day after day, and no matter how hard I tried, I couldn't get rid of this old man.

Everyone, try to imagine what it felt like for me to carry this strange old man every day; no matter how I tried, I couldn't get rid of him.

One day I found a large gourd, and I made some wine in it with grape juice. This wine was very good, it made my heart happy, and I sang a song all the way.

The old man saw me drinking the wine and saw how good the wine made me feel, so he gestured for me to give him some. After I gave it to him to drink, it made his head feel light, and he began to sing, shaking up and down even though he was still clinging to my neck.

Before long, his legs came off my neck, so I threw him violently to the ground and killed him by hitting him on the head with a large stone.

Commercial News

Finance: Conflicting News, Huge Fluctuations in Bid Premium 208

——Result: Continued Decline of Four and a Half Yuan——

At this time, the exchange market was stable, and the transactions in the market gradually became light. The market situation was calm for quite a long time. U.S. Cotton Near 1.2 Jiao 216

Yesterday, when the U.S. cotton market opened, due to profit-taking and foreign firm selling, all months fell by 2 to 4 pounds per point. There was spread selling in July contracts. And as the new and old harvests are similar, old cotton was transfered to new cotton. Afterwards, the market recovered due to short covering, buying by brokers, expectations of government purchases of spot cotton after selling off its stock, and a robust stock market. Government agents bought and market conditions were improving. Unofficial estimates indicate that the government sold 130,000 bales of government owned cotton. However, the amount of cotton the government purchased for future delivery was not close to this amount. Heth Estimates that mill use would be about 18,000 bales this week. Liverpool cotton reserves were 267,000 bales. The market close was firm. But, the market is currently wavering between the possibility of inflation and breaching the 1.2-jiao level, as a price of 1.2 jiao may trigger selling from stock holders and cotton syndicates. There is some talk of storage costs for the new cotton, but this will depend on the government's lending policy. Spot prices remain unchanged, futures prices up 3-10 points. English cotton spot prices were up 6 points, and futures were up 6-7 points. Indian cotton opened up firm with short covering and European export buying but retreated on profit taking. Pingle was up 1.25-2.125 rupees, Ormla was up 0.75-2.5 rupees, and White Luo Creek was up 2-4.25 rupees. Original telegraph as follows (10th dispatch):

Grains: Northern Merchants Compete for Near-Term Flour 217

Yesterday, after the flour market opened in the morning, the near-term months initially showed flat prices, followed by a sharp rise. With foreign wheat prices, Chicago had fallen back by about 3-4 jiao, and Canada improved by 1 jiao. When the market opened, the conflicting price trends in foreign wheat caused people to believe that prices would remain flat. However, after the second round of trading, prices gradually increased. Because the Northern merchants feared drought, those who manage grain were furiously buying. With new wheat about to come on the market in Jiangnan, foreign wheat prices were still cheap, and people acted nervously, exaggerating the situation. By the afternoon opening, the near-term market was still soaring, partly due to market sentiment, and partly due to the fact that flour inventories in various factories were truly depleted, so prices were repeatedly raised, even reaching 5 jiao 5.5 fen. Adding 5 fen to the standard price would bring it to the major level of 6 jiao. The seriousness of the situation should not be underestimated. The prices for June, July and August also rose sharply. The prices for September and October were relatively stable, as there were reports that factories continued to order a boatload of Australian wheat at a price of only 4 yuan 7 jiao 1 fen. Therefore, although buying was brisk, the price increase was less. As a result, the price for this month rose by 5 fen 2.5 li, the price for June rose by 3 fen 7 li, the price for July rose by 4 fen 2.5 li, the price for August rose by 3 fen 5 li, the price for September rose by 1 fen 2.5 li, and the price for October rose by 1 fen 7.5 li.

Customers Actively Buy Future Wheat at Higher Prices 218

Yesterday, the future wheat market showed flat prices in the morning, followed by a sharp rise in the afternoon. Foreign wheat prices in Chicago fell by about 3-4 jiao, and Canada improved by 1 jiao. After the market opened, the prices for various months were lower by 1-2 fen, because foreign wheat prices had decreased. By the close, the price trend of the flour market had greatly risen, which also led to higher prices. By the afternoon opening, due to concerns about the new wheat crop in the North being affected by drought, customers from other ports gradually increased their buying activity, so the market rose steadily. Based on this situation, it seems that the market should be rising, but the flow of foreign wheat continues, so an excessive price increase would be inappropriate. As a result, the prices for July and August each rose by 9 fen, and the price for September rose by 8 fen. The actual wheat market price is still stable, with Shandong wheat at 4 yuan 1 jiao, Henan wheat at 4 yuan, Haizhou wheat at 4 yuan 7 fen, and Jiangbei wheat at 3 yuan 9 jiao 7 fen. 4,000 bags of new wheat were shipped.

Chicago Wheat: According to Canadian government estimates, the Canadian harvest will be about 22.8 million bushels. Today, because the weather report was very good, the market bears softened slightly. Spot wheat and factory wheat also loosened. The U.S. government estimates that the U.S. winter wheat production will be 43.1 million bushels, slightly less than expected.

He Xia Rice Prices Continue to Fall by 0.2-0.3 Yuan 219

South Market Closed Today - Many Foreign Rice Shipments, Also Smaller

Local rice (Shanghai South) yesterday, the source of goods from various groups was similar to before, with a total of more than 30 firms arriving (a total of more than 6,000 shi). However, sales were sluggish, the situation was bleak, and the market was difficult to recover. The prices of various goods continued to decline. For example, Su Tong, Nan Gang and other japonica rice continued to depreciate by 0.2-0.3 yuan, while Qing Jiao and other late rice varieties were only purchased by the Qingdao group for over 300 bags, falling by more than 3 chi. Prices for other varieties such as Yin Bian Yuan also fell by 0.3-0.4 yuan. Today is the opening ceremony of the South Rice Merchants Association in the South Market, and all businesses are closed for the day.

(Shanghai North) Yesterday, 15-16 ships arrived from various routes in He Xia. The sales volume of various goods in the market was still weak, and the market price of white japonica rice also fell by about 0.1 yuan. Early thin rice prices fell by 0.1-0.2 yuan, white yuan also fell by a small amount, and other goods also appeared weak.

Foreign rice: Yesterday, the foreign rice market was characterized by a continuous stream of arriving ships and many orders still on the way. Traders, seeing that local inventory was sufficient and inland sales had decreased, were nervous and sold off cheaply, while importers, seeing that the market was weak, were hesitant to sell and waited for the market to improve before trading. Some customers, whose previous orders had not yet been fully loaded, were currently paying for existing inventory and temporarily stopped buying. Therefore, total spot sales of foreign rice for the day were less than 5,000 bags, and prices continued to fall by several fen to 0.1 yuan. Due to the large amount of arriving goods, the price of No. 3 rice from yesterday's Lu route fell to 8.9 yuan, which was about 0.15 yuan lower than the previous day. Yesterday, over 600 bags of ke xian rice were sold at a discount, and the price also decreased by a few fen. Among them, the Sichuan rice, which arrived in Shanghai a few days ago, was of excellent quality, similar to the high-quality rice from Jiangnan. The owner originally intended to store it and wait for a good price, and had previously offered several hundred bags at 10.04 yuan. However, due to the hot weather and the falling prices of foreign rice, they sold it along with the market, but because the goods were of higher quality, the sales were not sustained, and the price was able to stabilize, it is said.

New Broad Beans from Wenzhou on the Market 220

—New Goods Already Opening in Wuhu—

This year, the spring harvest season is favorable due to the sunny weather, and new goods are appearing on the market very early (last year it was at the end of the sixth lunar month). Yesterday, 300 bags of new broad beans from Wenzhou were on the market. The product is a small-grained variety, with only 70% dryness, and the price is 4 yuan. However, the merchants are taking a wait-and-see approach, so there is no rush to raise prices for the new goods. Because the bean quality is too soft, the East Asian group is not buying, and the Tianjin group has no space for transportation and loading, so no transactions have been made. The new rapeseed was launched the day before yesterday for 10,000 bags from Wuhu, for delivery in June-July, calculated according to the standard regulations of 3 jin bags, not accounting for the merchant's scale. The price is between 3 liang 8 qian and 8 qian. Currently, the weather is good, and the harvest year appears to be plentiful, so the market sentiment is bearish.

Local Spot Cotton Inventory Thickens, Silk and Tea: Red and Green Tea Arrive in Abundance 221

Yesterday, more than 2,000 boxes of red tea from Qimen, Ningzhou, and Zhide were continuously shipped from the Yangtze River and Hangzhou routes. More than 800 packages of green tea from Huzhou and Ningbo were also shipped to Shanghai. Both red and green tea arrivals are very abundant, but the market transactions are still weak. Zhen Mei green tea from Sui'an has been launched by Tong Fu Foreign Firm for 120 yuan. It is said that more than 700 boxes have been stranded in the market, and the tea prices are likely to continue to decline.
